<div id="review_902333357" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/902333357" />
    <a title="Noël Cades" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28797021-no-l-cades"><img alt="Noël Cades" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442973197p2/28797021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/902333357?book_show_action=true">Apr 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Noël Cades" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Noël Cades" href="/user/show/28797021-no-l-cades">Noël Cades</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28797021-no-l-cades?shelf=older-man">older-man</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28797021-no-l-cades?shelf=student-teacher-relationship">student-teacher-relationship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28797021-no-l-cades?shelf=student-teacher">student-teacher</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer902333357" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3619485015765982413">This is a very well-written and intense book, that will disturb and likely disappoint readers looking for a happy romance. Those looking for a challenging and engrossing read, with interesting and complex characters, will find much to absorb them.<br/><br/>Sarah is only 14 when she embarks on a sado-masochistic sexual relationship with her 38-year-old English teacher Daniel Carr. (Bear in mind that the book is set in Australia, where the age of consent is 16 and perspectives on underage sex are considerab</span>
  <span id="freeText3619485015765982413" style="display:none">This is a very well-written and intense book, that will disturb and likely disappoint readers looking for a happy romance. Those looking for a challenging and engrossing read, with interesting and complex characters, will find much to absorb them.<br /><br />Sarah is only 14 when she embarks on a sado-masochistic sexual relationship with her 38-year-old English teacher Daniel Carr. (Bear in mind that the book is set in Australia, where the age of consent is 16 and perspectives on underage sex are considerably different than in the US). Daniel Carr then deserts her and her life goes to pieces for the next seven years, when they finally reunite. He is arguably more destroyed by the relationship than she is but it is highly destructive on both sides.<br /><br />Taming the Beast is about the forbidden and the destructive power of love and sex. It features complicated and illegal relationships and mature activity. If you are of a sensitive disposition or easily offended, just skip it, it's not for you.<br /><br />If you can cope with an interesting and harrowing read, and one that is also very gritty and realistic compared to many coming-of-age and "student teacher" novels, then there is much of interest here.<br /><br />It's an enthralling read and will leave you as conflicted as Nabokov's Lolita may do. The heroine clearly starts out as a victim, but what is she by the end of the book? Has she reclaimed her agency? </span>
  <a data-text-id="3619485015765982413" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText14096202024807502505" style="display:none">3.5 star rating<br /><br />Wow. Honestly I don't even know what to say or what to feel. Right now I am odd and hurt because of the ending in this book-or this book period. Don't worry I will not spoil anything for you guys!<br /><br />This is a dark dark and very twisted story but what I like about this was that the author did not give a predictable ending/A predictable story either.<br /><br />For myself I think that the book is OK writing wise. It uses a lot of literature and that's what I like most about it is the literature used it. But for me personally I thought it was an OK book within OK story. I like dark erotic books, really I do, but this one pushes my limits a bit. <br /><br />The characters are written well for how they were supposed to be portrayed. My favorite character was Jamie actually. Sarah was an interesting character.<br /><br />Overall of the book was OK. Not really for me entirely. Well I read this author again? Really I do not know. I feel as though a story like this, and how she portrayed it is a hit or miss.<br /><br />3.5 stars</span>

<div id="review_345705460" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/345705460" />
    <a title="Lindsay" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9594561-lindsay"><img alt="Lindsay" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1338651088p2/9594561.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/345705460?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lindsay" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lindsay" href="/user/show/9594561-lindsay">Lindsay</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer345705460" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6270561825018111105">I was absolutely captivated by this book. I don't think it deserves the low reviews it has been given purely because of the subject matter. It is a raw and honest portrayal of an obsessive, possessive and destructive relationship. I think that Emily Maguire did a beautiful job in writing the story with such realism even if it is at times shocking and unnerving. I think that some people who have rated it lowly struggle to believe that such relationships exist, but there are couples who do behave </span>
  <span id="freeText6270561825018111105" style="display:none">I was absolutely captivated by this book. I don't think it deserves the low reviews it has been given purely because of the subject matter. It is a raw and honest portrayal of an obsessive, possessive and destructive relationship. I think that Emily Maguire did a beautiful job in writing the story with such realism even if it is at times shocking and unnerving. I think that some people who have rated it lowly struggle to believe that such relationships exist, but there are couples who do behave so violently and damagingly towards each other as an unfortunate byproduct of the extremity of their feelings for each other.<br />This novel powerfully demonstrated the depths to which a harrowingly intense love can sink. It made me angry, it made me hurt, it made me cry and any writer who can evoke such strong emotions through their words deserves serious credit in my opinion.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6270561825018111105" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zs1v22xsasV32eiqVWsQJaJglR4ydRU836361UOg9nOCOxBd+LQXAvtT7NsaABu/kD/9aIR9XapaBcuwGDZBag==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('XtzokzZDmZLjtdEAUMAang2pyFjt8keVp9Hlzo74qrkSKpcVopvkVW8/1XEfqxEEP/agLlv6DwMiedSr1W4doA==')})
  }
//]]>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/277741-taming-the-beast">Quotes from Taming the Beast</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;That's what Jamie didn't understand: it was never just sex. Even the fastest, dirtiest, most impersonal screw was about more than sex. It was about connection. It was about looking at another human being and seeing your own loneliness and neediness reflected back. It was recognising that together you had the power to temporarily banish that sense of isolation. It was about experiencing what it was to be human at the basest, most instinctive level. How could that be described as just anything?&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/255910-that-s-what-jamie-didn-t-understand-it-was-never-just-sex">135 likes</a>

          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;But then, life is a constant withering of possibilities. Some are stolen with the lives of people you love. Others are let go, with regret and reluctance and deep, deep sorrow. But there is compensation for lives unlived in the intoxicating joy of knowing that the life you have - right here, right now - if the one you have chosen. There is power in that, and hope.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
